
-----title
清河 (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1ed2d2b5105342a7b228edcc6731ebf4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1ed2d2b5105342a7b228edcc6731ebf4");'><span id='1ed2d2b5105342a7b228edcc6731ebf4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=653&endYear=675')">653-675年</a>，1-23岁</div><div id='1ed2d2b5105342a7b228edcc6731ebf4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=653&endYear=653')">653年</a>　是年崔融生，郡望清河武城。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=654&endYear=675')">654-675年</a>　是年具体活动不详，或居家清河，姑系于此。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
西安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='354a16e9ab654417932dfe39c266454a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("354a16e9ab654417932dfe39c266454a");'><span id='354a16e9ab654417932dfe39c266454a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=676&endYear=679')">676-679年</a>，24-27岁</div><div id='354a16e9ab654417932dfe39c266454a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=676&endYear=676')">676年1月</a>　是年正月，应辞殚文律科制举，及第。此后，与李峤、苏味道、杜审言等交游，被称为“文章四友”世号“崔、李、苏、杜”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=677&endYear=677')">677年</a>　去年、今年、明年连年应举，连中八科。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=677&endYear=677')">677年</a>　释褐为绛州夏县尉。李峤在京兆府三原县尉任，遭诬枉，得以洗刷清白。夏，访崔融未遇。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=678&endYear=678')">678年</a>　连年登科，累补东宫左春坊宫门丞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=679&endYear=679')">679年</a>　是年在任，姑系于此。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='435eac5cce404fca9ce774500bbab4a1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("435eac5cce404fca9ce774500bbab4a1");'><span id='435eac5cce404fca9ce774500bbab4a1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=681&endYear=682')">681-682年</a>，29-30岁</div><div id='435eac5cce404fca9ce774500bbab4a1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=681&endYear=681')">681年</a>　是年在宫门丞任。薛元超表荐为崇文馆直学士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=681&endYear=681')">681年10月</a>　本月，参议吏部、兵部选事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=682&endYear=682')">682年</a>　是年在宫门丞兼崇文馆直学士任，兼太子侍读。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='81247a33721f45a58dfbea7749ab2eac_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("81247a33721f45a58dfbea7749ab2eac");'><span id='81247a33721f45a58dfbea7749ab2eac_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=684&endYear=684')">684年</a>，32岁</div><div id='81247a33721f45a58dfbea7749ab2eac' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=684&endYear=684')">684年</a>　是年吏部尚书韦待价摄司空，为高宗乾陵山陵使，辟为从事。有表。作品：《为裴尚书慰山陵事毕上表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（原文此处，年龄误记为“三十七岁”，实为“三十二岁”。）</span><div id='poem_1364607' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364607' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364607?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为裴尚书慰山陵事毕上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（684年）</span><span class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364607_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364607'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364607'>臣某等言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364607_comment'></div>自遏密缠悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364607_comment'></div>山陵启卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364607_comment'></div>陛下情深撤帐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364607_comment'></div>恋切游冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364607_comment'></div>至于卤簿吉凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364607_comment'></div>途程日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364607_comment'></div>莫不亲垂睿旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364607_comment'></div>显发宸衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364607_comment'></div>由是川后竞驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364607_comment'></div>山祇荐委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364607_comment'></div>云物澄霁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364607_comment'></div>景气清和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364607_comment'></div>灵骖电转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364607_comment'></div>非因下人之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364607_comment'></div>神辇风行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364607_comment'></div>自有上天之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364607_comment'></div>山河道路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364607_comment'></div>曾不艰虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364607_comment'></div>木石犬马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364607_comment'></div>咸当感悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364607_comment'></div>岂非大孝所洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364607_comment'></div>通于神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364607_comment'></div>至圣所宏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364607_comment'></div>动于天地者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364607_comment'></div>伏以某日吉辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364607_comment'></div>永安神寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364607_comment'></div>郊原四合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364607_comment'></div>门阙九重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364607_comment'></div>傍奉园林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364607_comment'></div>近瞻京邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364607_comment'></div>元宫一閟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364607_comment'></div>紫禁长辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364607_comment'></div>万国同轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364607_comment'></div>五情分裂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364607_comment'></div>伏惟皇太后陛下哀慕永往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364607_comment'></div>圣怀难居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364607_comment'></div>臣等早侍轩墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364607_comment'></div>谬沾簪履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364607_comment'></div>攀龙不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364607_comment'></div>顾慕轩辕之台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364607_comment'></div>耘鸟相惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364607_comment'></div>屏营会稽之野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364607_comment'></div>限以归从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364607_comment'></div>末由诣阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364607_comment'></div>无任悲感之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364607_comment'></div>谨遣某奉表以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1364607_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=684&endYear=684')">684年12月2日</a>　此日，薛元超卒。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
登封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ced0458e1ddd4b1d96d206c5bf7b187b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ced0458e1ddd4b1d96d206c5bf7b187b");'><span id='ced0458e1ddd4b1d96d206c5bf7b187b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=680&endYear=680')">680年</a>，28岁</div><div id='ced0458e1ddd4b1d96d206c5bf7b187b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=680&endYear=680')">680年2月</a>　是年在宫门丞任。二月，高宗幸嵩山，亲谒少姨庙、启母庙，命树碑，承诏作《嵩山启母庙碑》<div id='poem_1364620' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364620' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364620?labeling=true' target='_blank'>嵩山启母庙碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（680年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14914, "初唐", "崔融", "poem_title_1364620")'>崔融</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364620_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364620'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364620'>臣闻天地生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364620_comment'></div>其法自然之谓道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364620_comment'></div>阴阳鼓舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364620_comment'></div>其功不测之谓神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364620_comment'></div>然则物或类感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364620_comment'></div>事因通变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364620_comment'></div>乾栋倾而三光北驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364620_comment'></div>坤舆缺而百川东泻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364620_comment'></div>河沦越雟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364620_comment'></div>有郡邑之为鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364620_comment'></div>水陷阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364620_comment'></div>有吏人之化鳖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364620_comment'></div>访遗踪于女峡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364620_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1364620", 1364620, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>风雨萧条</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364620_comment'></div>徵往事于姑泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364620_comment'></div>弦歌响亮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364620_comment'></div>盈虚靡定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364620_comment'></div>合散焉常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364620_comment'></div>不知谁子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364620_comment'></div>既老氏之多懵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364620_comment'></div>忽然为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364620_comment'></div>宁贾生之足辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364620_comment'></div>仰观俯察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364620_comment'></div>裁识幽明之故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364620_comment'></div>原始反终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364620_comment'></div>未穷生死之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364620_comment'></div>得于道而失于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364620_comment'></div>义有必然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364620_comment'></div>出于机而入于机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364620_comment'></div>理无或废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364620_comment'></div>知变化者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364620_comment'></div>其知神之所为乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364620_comment'></div>臣谨按启母庙者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364620_comment'></div>盖夏后启之母也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364620_comment'></div>汉避景帝讳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364620_comment'></div>改启之字曰开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364620_comment'></div>厥后相传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364620_comment'></div>或为开母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364620_comment'></div>而顾野王舆地志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364620_comment'></div>卢元明嵩高记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364620_comment'></div>并不寻避讳之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364620_comment'></div>以为阳翟妇人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364620_comment'></div>事不经见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364620_comment'></div>谅无所取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364620_comment'></div>粤若玉斗璇玑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364620_comment'></div>李母之居邻北极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364620_comment'></div>金台石室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364620_comment'></div>王母之宅在西山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364620_comment'></div>气为母则群物以萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364620_comment'></div>月为母则容光必照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364620_comment'></div>坤为母则上下交泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364620_comment'></div>后为母则邦家有成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364620_comment'></div>故华胥履迹而雄氏孕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364620_comment'></div>女登感神而炎运作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364620_comment'></div>星流华渚而白帝生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364620_comment'></div>月贯幽房而黑精降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364620_comment'></div>明明有夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364620_comment'></div>穆穆涂山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364620_comment'></div>予娶于度土之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364620_comment'></div>女婚于台桑之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364620_comment'></div>搜奇帝纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364620_comment'></div>摭异归藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364620_comment'></div>束生发蒙而有迷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364620_comment'></div>韩子称贤而不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364620_comment'></div>汉臣之笔墨泉海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364620_comment'></div>陈其令名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364620_comment'></div>秦相之一字千金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364620_comment'></div>叙其嘉应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364620_comment'></div>士歌南国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364620_comment'></div>徒闻禹之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364620_comment'></div>石破北方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364620_comment'></div>终见生余之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364620_comment'></div>则郭璞所谓阳城西启母石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364620_comment'></div>李肜所谓嵩山南启母祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364620_comment'></div>隋巢之说有徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364620_comment'></div>鸿烈之言无爽者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364620_comment'></div>昔者鸾川之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364620_comment'></div>母变空桑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364620_comment'></div>豚水之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364620_comment'></div>男生破竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364620_comment'></div>美人之虹名螮蝀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364620_comment'></div>仙妇之月作蟾蜍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364620_comment'></div>精卫衔木而偿冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364620_comment'></div>女尸化草而成殡<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作媚）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364620_comment'></div>山崩蜀道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364620_comment'></div>台妇而无归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364620_comment'></div>石立武昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364620_comment'></div>亭望夫而不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364620_comment'></div>论乎诞载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364620_comment'></div>群下莫尊于帝王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364620_comment'></div>语乎迁易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364620_comment'></div>凡百无闻于感致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364620_comment'></div>美矣哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364620_comment'></div>不可得而称也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364620_comment'></div>大唐革去故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364620_comment'></div>鼎取新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364620_comment'></div>与运而生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364620_comment'></div>继天而作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364620_comment'></div>握乾坤而造物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364620_comment'></div>海内知春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364620_comment'></div>辟混沌而为家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364620_comment'></div>域中无外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364620_comment'></div>天皇膺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364620_comment'></div>数顺讴歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364620_comment'></div>金匮玉版。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364620_comment'></div>服皇王之能事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364620_comment'></div>衢室庙堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364620_comment'></div>承祖宗之茂烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364620_comment'></div>垂衣裳而作元后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364620_comment'></div>端拱北辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364620_comment'></div>负黼扆而朝诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364620_comment'></div>向明南面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364620_comment'></div>周邦赫赫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364620_comment'></div>其道洽于成康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364620_comment'></div>汉室巍巍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364620_comment'></div>其化钟于文景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364620_comment'></div>东渐西被。<div id='poem_sentence_350_1364620_comment'></div>终惭神女之工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_351_1364620_comment'></div>敢作铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_352_1364620_comment'></div></div><div 泾川

class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364611_comment'></div>加帛不暖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364611_comment'></div>比者西京有宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364611_comment'></div>老母在堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364611_comment'></div>臣以留司之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364611_comment'></div>尚接和颜之半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364611_comment'></div>贪荣徇禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364611_comment'></div>惟迫于甘旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364595_comment'></div>果得非常之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364595_comment'></div>伏见某日敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364595_comment'></div>虢州阌乡县界老君见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364595_comment'></div>并授邬元宗语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364595_comment'></div>皤然<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1364595", 1364595, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>鹤首</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364595_comment'></div>至哉龙德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364595_comment'></div>若游涡水之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364595_comment'></div>疑往流沙之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364595_comment'></div>叙皇威之有截。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364595_comment'></div>论国祚之无疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364595_comment'></div>道可以济天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364595_comment'></div>功可以侔造化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364595_comment'></div>元言妙键。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364595_comment'></div>关令受教而先迷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364595_comment'></div>神理希微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364595_comment'></div>河公愿谈而莫测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364595_comment'></div>方验老人见于南极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364595_comment'></div>但谓承天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364595_comment'></div>黄人游于后池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364595_comment'></div>止云乘土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364595_comment'></div>固不可同年而议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364595_comment'></div>臣等豫睹嘉祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364595_comment'></div>早参簪笏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364595_comment'></div>惟神降福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364595_comment'></div>欣承帝系之隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364595_comment'></div>惟德洞冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364595_comment'></div>愿奉元元之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364595_comment'></div>无任感悦之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364595_comment'></div>谨附某奉表称贺以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1364595_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
临夏州

id='poem_sentence_20_46390'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_46390_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=688&endYear=688')">688年</a>　是年为安息行军大总管韦待价掌书记，在西北边塞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=688&endYear=688')">688年</a>　为韦待价撰文。作品：《代宰相上尊号表》《为韦右相贺平贼表》<div id='poem_1364574' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364574' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364574?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代宰相上尊号表</a><span class='authorDate'>（688年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14914, "初唐", "崔融", "poem_title_1364574")'>崔融</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364574_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364574'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364574'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364574_comment'></div>臣闻形器以陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364574_comment'></div>万物有名之谓母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364574_comment'></div>尊卑既位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364574_comment'></div>两仪合德之谓皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364574_comment'></div>非母则不能慈爱域中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364574_comment'></div>非皇则不能导化天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364574_comment'></div>历考前政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364574_comment'></div>详窥旧牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364574_comment'></div>金匮玉版。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364574_comment'></div>帝王之迹易推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364574_comment'></div>铁轴铜浑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364574_comment'></div>天地之情可验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364574_comment'></div>不知谁子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364574_comment'></div>气母握其灵机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364574_comment'></div>厥初生人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364574_comment'></div>维皇启其光宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364574_comment'></div>然则仪坤配永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364574_comment'></div>至圣者所以降天符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364574_comment'></div>建极施尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364574_comment'></div>至神者所以塞人望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364574_comment'></div>礼存知贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364574_comment'></div>事叶强为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364574_comment'></div>天命则休应毕臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364574_comment'></div>人心则休应允集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364574_comment'></div>不可得而避也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364574_comment'></div>不可得而违也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364574_comment'></div>其唯圣人乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364574_comment'></div>其唯神用乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364574_comment'></div>伏见某日制书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364574_comment'></div>以天授圣图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364574_comment'></div>群臣上尊号曰圣母神皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364574_comment'></div>昭备典册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364574_comment'></div>肃应景命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364574_comment'></div>大赦天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364574_comment'></div>赐酺五日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364574_comment'></div>含生之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364574_comment'></div>禀识之俦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364574_comment'></div>雍雍如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364574_comment'></div>欣欣如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364574_comment'></div>洎鸟兽率舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364574_comment'></div>与草树咸乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364574_comment'></div>中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364574_comment'></div>臣闻以凡测圣者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364574_comment'></div>理绝于名言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364574_comment'></div>以管窥天者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364574_comment'></div>事迷于远近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364574_comment'></div>虽帝其何力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364574_comment'></div>自闻田父之歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364574_comment'></div>而事有不谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364574_comment'></div>终获樵夫之笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364574_comment'></div>亦安敢梗概而无述哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364574_comment'></div>粤若稽古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364574_comment'></div>圣母神皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364574_comment'></div>阴阳和而睿德生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364574_comment'></div>日月合而冲灵降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364574_comment'></div>其在家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364574_comment'></div>御娀氏之瑶台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364574_comment'></div>其正位也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364574_comment'></div>绾汉皇之玉玺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364574_comment'></div>维皇高祖肇创王业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364574_comment'></div>惟太宗克成帝功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364574_comment'></div>惟高宗发挥二圣之耿光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364574_comment'></div>惟陛下对越三后之明命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364574_comment'></div>显承遗托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364574_comment'></div>敬守前基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364574_comment'></div>宏济艰难。<div id='poem_sentence_68_1364574_comment'></div>义切园陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364574_comment'></div>其至公有如此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364574_comment'></div>七月而葬。<div id='poem_sentence_73_1364574_comment'></div>载怀高蹈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364574_comment'></div>陛下致还君之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364574_comment'></div>德盛于谦尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364574_comment'></div>皇帝竭为子之孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364574_comment'></div>诚深于覆育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364574_comment'></div>八纮无外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364574_comment'></div>六合一家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364574_comment'></div>其冲让有如此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364574_comment'></div>蒐八代之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364574_comment'></div>讲三王之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364574_comment'></div>定齐斩之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364574_comment'></div>革靡曼之音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364574_comment'></div>草章程。<div id='poem_sentence_88_1364574_comment'></div>议<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_89_1364574", 1364574, "Clauses/89/Comments/0")'>故误</span>之条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364574_comment'></div>百官以理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364574_comment'></div>万人以察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364574_comment'></div>其制作有如此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364574_comment'></div>慎终追远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364574_comment'></div>因心罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364574_comment'></div>崇七庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364574_comment'></div>广三雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364574_comment'></div>仁不遗于一物。<div id='poem_sentence_99_1364574_comment'></div>训甲兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364574_comment'></div>誓将帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364574_comment'></div>南北清宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364574_comment'></div>东西缉穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364574_comment'></div>有轩皇战伐之功焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364574_comment'></div>定都邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364574_comment'></div>殊徽号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364574_comment'></div>居三统之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364574_comment'></div>处六合之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364574_comment'></div>有周成隆平之业焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364574_comment'></div>锦绣罗縠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364574_comment'></div>雕文刻镂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364574_comment'></div>人君之美色也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364574_comment'></div>而陛下浣濯之服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364574_comment'></div>大帛之衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364574_comment'></div>珍羞圆方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364574_comment'></div>滋味重累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364574_comment'></div>人君之甘旨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364574_comment'></div>而陛下藜藿之羹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364574_comment'></div>粢粝之饭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364574_comment'></div>黄金白玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364574_comment'></div>青珠紫贝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364574_comment'></div>人君之骄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364574_comment'></div>而陛下所宝惟贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364574_comment'></div>所重惟谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364574_comment'></div>上林禁苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364574_comment'></div>层台累榭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364574_comment'></div>人君之丽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364574_comment'></div>而陛下宫垣不葺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364574_comment'></div>廊宇莫修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364574_comment'></div>置拾遗补阙之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364574_comment'></div>则前疑后承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364574_comment'></div>仰天俯地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364574_comment'></div>孰云尚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364574_comment'></div>创通贤招谏之匦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364574_comment'></div>则听声之鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364574_comment'></div>告善之旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364574_comment'></div>畴以懿兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364574_comment'></div>夫然后不登而高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364574_comment'></div>不行而远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364574_comment'></div>天降以瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364574_comment'></div>地升以符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364574_comment'></div>日月光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364574_comment'></div>风雨润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364574_comment'></div>庆云出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364574_comment'></div>神泉涌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364574_comment'></div>凤凰翔于庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364574_comment'></div>麒麟臻于囿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364574_comment'></div>云集雾散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364574_comment'></div>日至月书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364574_comment'></div>固不可得而言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364574_comment'></div>陛下犹固守冲挹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364574_comment'></div>深惟惕厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364574_comment'></div>以元默为神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364574_comment'></div>澹泊为德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364574_comment'></div>回圣虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364574_comment'></div>运全谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364574_comment'></div>采衢室之旧仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364574_comment'></div>酌明台之故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364574_comment'></div>因人之欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364574_comment'></div>不日而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364574_comment'></div>于是灵命孔彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364574_comment'></div>元心总集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364574_comment'></div>山开秘篆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364574_comment'></div>洛出祥图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364574_comment'></div>每缨冕同观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364574_comment'></div>轩墀共谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364574_comment'></div>则有曦车五色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364574_comment'></div>对玉匣而如迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364574_comment'></div>云盖三层。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364574_comment'></div>伴琼缄而不去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364574_comment'></div>岂非显见神物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364574_comment'></div>觉寤黎蒸者欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364574_comment'></div>可以昭报昊穹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364574_comment'></div>可以抑扬宗社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364574_comment'></div>明至德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364574_comment'></div>表至功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364574_comment'></div>阴阳不测之谓神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364574_comment'></div>应变不穷之谓圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364574_comment'></div>洋洋乎发育万物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364574_comment'></div>荡荡乎人无能名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1364574_comment'></div>尊号之来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364574_comment'></div>岂徒然而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1364574_comment'></div>圣母神皇乃不得已而从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364574_comment'></div>命有司膺大礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364574_comment'></div>秩群望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364574_comment'></div>怀百神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364574_comment'></div>配诸侯于四渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364574_comment'></div>视上公于五镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364574_comment'></div>百姓有罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364574_comment'></div>思与天下涤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1364574_comment'></div>一人有庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1364574_comment'></div>思与天下覃之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1364574_comment'></div>垂动钥之深思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1364574_comment'></div>降合钱之普泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1364574_comment'></div>凡百在宥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1364574_comment'></div>不知手之舞之足之蹈之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1364574_comment'></div>岂使女娲神化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1364574_comment'></div>仍参泰古之皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1364574_comment'></div>太姒徽音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1364574_comment'></div>独擅隆周之母而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1364574_comment'></div>微臣早沾扬历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1364574_comment'></div>亟奉恩荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1364574_comment'></div>惭拥肿之曲材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1364574_comment'></div>荷生成之大德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1364574_comment'></div>山涛者浑金之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1364574_comment'></div>魏国擢之以尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1364574_comment'></div>伊尹者饰玉之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1364574_comment'></div>殷朝待之于右相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1364574_comment'></div>在臣驽暗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1364574_comment'></div>远谢贤明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1364574_comment'></div>徼逢振拭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1364574_comment'></div>擢登左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1364574_comment'></div>陛下不以臣不肖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1364574_comment'></div>复使臣待罪元戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1364574_comment'></div>顾无平虏之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1364574_comment'></div>未荅破羌之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1364574_comment'></div>恭闻瑞典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1364574_comment'></div>载沐鸿私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1364574_comment'></div>幸属皇羲之代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1364574_comment'></div>欣承帝魁之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1364574_comment'></div>冕旒端拱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1364574_comment'></div>既不获接景前行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1364574_comment'></div>玉帛来朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1364574_comment'></div>又不获趋风后位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1364574_comment'></div>横行万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1364574_comment'></div>限中国以长城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1364574_comment'></div>悚踊一隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1364574_comment'></div>望东朝于西域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1364574_comment'></div>不任悦豫翘勤之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1364574_comment'></div>谨遣某官奉表称贺以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_230_1364574_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364606?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为韦右相贺平贼表</a><span class='authorDate'>（688年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14914, "初唐", "崔融", "poem_title_1364606")'>崔融</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364606_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364606'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364606'>臣某言。伏奉某月日递敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364606_comment'></div>逆贼等并已传首都市。幕庭拜受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364606_comment'></div>旌门宣告。凡预军司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364606_comment'></div>孰不庆悦。中贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364606_comment'></div>臣闻恶禽怪兽。有以彰普覆之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364606_comment'></div>乱臣逆子。不能损盛明之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364606_comment'></div>故三监作难。周王未寝于颂声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364606_comment'></div>七国为灾。汉帝克臻于刑措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364606_comment'></div>伏惟圣母神皇陛下象天之运。法地之安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364606_comment'></div>泽浸河海。光悬日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364606_comment'></div>以忠信为甲冑。以慈惠为干戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364606_comment'></div>所向无前。何人不服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364606_comment'></div>举神兵如电扫。破凶党若冰离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364606_comment'></div>数月妖氛。一朝清荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364606_comment'></div>斯实皇威远肃。圣化傍沾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364606_comment'></div>故能市不改肆。人皆安堵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364606_comment'></div>臣滥承天泽。忝预戎麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364606_comment'></div>闻逆命而增愤。听枭悬而累抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364606_comment'></div>庆快之情。倍百恒品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364606_comment'></div>不任悦豫之至。谨附某官奉表称贺以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364606_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1364606_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=688&endYear=688')">688年12月25日</a>　此日，从武后拜洛受图，令撰《洛出宝图颂》以进。<br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_1_46387'>万里度<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作照）</span>关山，苍茫非一状。<div id='poem_sentence_1_46387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_46389_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_46389'>河水日东注，河源乃西极。<div id='poem_sentence_1_46389_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_46389'>思君正如此，谁为生羽翼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_46389_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_46389'>日夕大川阴，云霞千里色。<div class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/46388?labeling=true' target='_blank'>西征军行遇风</a><span class='authorDate'>（688年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14914, "初唐", "崔融", "poem_title_46388")'>崔融</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_46388_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_46388'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_46388'>北风卷尘沙，左右不相识。<div id='poem_sentence_0_46388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_46388'>飒飒吹万里，昏昏同一色。<div id='poem_sentence_1_46388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_46388'>马烦莫敢进，人急<span id='poem_sentence_6_46388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_46388'>兵气腾北荒，军声振<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作重）</span>西极。<div id='poem_sentence_7_46388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_46388'>坐觉威灵远，行看氛祲息。<div id='poem_sentence_8_46388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' "poem_allusion_46385")'>寻河</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4472, "poem_allusion_46385")'>营门柳</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5681, id='poem_sentence_0_46385'>穹庐杂种乱金方，武将神兵下玉堂。<div id='poem_sentence_0_46385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_46385'>天子旌旗过细柳，匈奴运数尽枯杨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_46385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_46385'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_46385", 46385, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>关头</span>落月横西岭，塞下凝云断北荒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_46385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_46385'>漠漠边尘飞众鸟，昏昏朔气聚群羊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_46385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_46385'>依稀蜀杖迷新竹，髣髴胡床识故桑。<div id='poem_sentence_4_46385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_46385'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5681, "poem_sentence_5_46385")'>临海</span>旧来闻骠骑，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3886, "poem_sentence_5_46385")'>寻河</span>本自有中郎。<div id='poem_sentence_5_46385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_46385'>坐看战壁为平土，近待军营作破羌。<div id='poem_sentence_6_46385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_46385'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_46385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/46375?labeling=true' target='_blank'>塞上<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作北）</span>寄内</a><span class='authorDate'>（688年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14914, "初唐", "崔融", "poem_title_46375")'>崔融</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_46375_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_46375'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_46375'>旅魂惊塞北，归望断河西。<div id='poem_sentence_0_46375_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_46375'>春风若可寄，暂为绕兰闺。<div id='poem_sentence_1_46375_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_46375'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_46375_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=688&endYear=688')">688年</a>　是年有文。作品：《代宰相上尊号表》《为韦右相贺平贼表》《进洛图颂表》《为朝集使于思言等请封中岳表》<div id='poem_1364574' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364574' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364574?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代宰相上尊号表</a><span class='authorDate'>（688年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14914, "初唐", "崔融", "poem_title_1364574")'>崔融</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364574_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364574'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364574'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364574_comment'></div>臣闻形器以陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364574_comment'></div>万物有名之谓母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364574_comment'></div>尊卑既位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364574_comment'></div>两仪合德之谓皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364574_comment'></div>非母则不能慈爱域中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364574_comment'></div>非皇则不能导化天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364574_comment'></div>历考前政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364574_comment'></div>详窥旧牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364574_comment'></div>金匮玉版。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364574_comment'></div>帝王之迹易推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364574_comment'></div>铁轴铜浑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364574_comment'></div>天地之情可验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364574_comment'></div>不知谁子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364574_comment'></div>气母握其灵机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364574_comment'></div>厥初生人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364574_comment'></div>维皇启其光宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364574_comment'></div>然则仪坤配永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364574_comment'></div>至圣者所以降天符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364574_comment'></div>建极施尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364574_comment'></div>至神者所以塞人望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364574_comment'></div>礼存知贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364574_comment'></div>事叶强为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364574_comment'></div>天命则休应毕臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364574_comment'></div>人心则休应允集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364574_comment'></div>不可得而避也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364574_comment'></div>不可得而违也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364574_comment'></div>其唯圣人乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364574_comment'></div>其唯神用乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364574_comment'></div>伏见某日制书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364574_comment'></div>以天授圣图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364574_comment'></div>群臣上尊号曰圣母神皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364574_comment'></div>昭备典册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364574_comment'></div>肃应景命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364574_comment'></div>大赦天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364574_comment'></div>赐酺五日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364574_comment'></div>含生之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364574_comment'></div>禀识之俦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364574_comment'></div>雍雍如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364574_comment'></div>欣欣如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364574_comment'></div>洎鸟兽率舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364574_comment'></div>与草树咸乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364574_comment'></div>中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364574_comment'></div>臣闻以凡测圣者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364574_comment'></div>理绝于名言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364574_comment'></div>以管窥天者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364574_comment'></div>事迷于远近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364574_comment'></div>虽帝其何力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364574_comment'></div>自闻田父之歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364574_comment'></div>而事有不谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364574_comment'></div>终获樵夫之笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364574_comment'></div>亦安敢梗概而无述哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364574_comment'></div>粤若稽古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364574_comment'></div>圣母神皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364574_comment'></div>阴阳和而睿德生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364574_comment'></div>日月合而冲灵降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364574_comment'></div>其在家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364574_comment'></div>御娀氏之瑶台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364574_comment'></div>其正位也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364574_comment'></div>绾汉皇之玉玺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364574_comment'></div>维皇高祖肇创王业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364574_comment'></div>惟太宗克成帝功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364574_comment'></div>惟高宗发挥二圣之耿光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364574_comment'></div>惟陛下对越三后之明命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364574_comment'></div>显承遗托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364574_comment'></div>敬守前基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364574_comment'></div>宏济艰难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364574_comment'></div>躬亲政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364574_comment'></div>情深社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364574_comment'></div>义切园陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364574_comment'></div>其至公有如此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364574_comment'></div>七月而葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364574_comment'></div>三年免丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364574_comment'></div>乃顾明辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364574_comment'></div>载怀高蹈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364574_comment'></div>陛下致还君之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364574_comment'></div>德盛于谦尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364574_comment'></div>皇帝竭为子之孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364574_comment'></div>诚深于覆育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364574_comment'></div>八纮无外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364574_comment'></div>六合一家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364574_comment'></div>其冲让有如此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364574_comment'></div>蒐八代之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364574_comment'></div>讲三王之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364574_comment'></div>定齐斩之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364574_comment'></div>革靡曼之音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364574_comment'></div>草章程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364574_comment'></div>垂劝诫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364574_comment'></div>除指斥之坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364574_comment'></div>议<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_89_1364574", 1364574, "Clauses/89/Comments/0")'>故误</span>之条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364574_comment'></div>百官以理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364574_comment'></div>万人以察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364574_comment'></div>其制作有如此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364574_comment'></div>慎终追远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364574_comment'></div>因心罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364574_comment'></div>崇七庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364574_comment'></div>广三雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364574_comment'></div>仁不遗于一物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364574_comment'></div>教必行于百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364574_comment'></div>有虞舜大孝之德焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364574_comment'></div>训甲兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364574_comment'></div>誓将帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364574_comment'></div>南北清宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364574_comment'></div>东西缉穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364574_comment'></div>有轩皇战伐之功焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364574_comment'></div>定都邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364574_comment'></div>殊徽号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364574_comment'></div>居三统之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364574_comment'></div>处六合之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364574_comment'></div>有周成隆平之业焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364574_comment'></div>锦绣罗縠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364574_comment'></div>雕文刻镂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364574_comment'></div>人君之美色也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364574_comment'></div>而陛下浣濯之服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364574_comment'></div>大帛之衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364574_comment'></div>珍羞圆方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364574_comment'></div>滋味重累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364574_comment'></div>人君之甘旨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364574_comment'></div>而陛下藜藿之羹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364574_comment'></div>粢粝之饭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364574_comment'></div>黄金白玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364574_comment'></div>青珠紫贝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364574_comment'></div>人君之骄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364574_comment'></div>而陛下所宝惟贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364574_comment'></div>所重惟谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364574_comment'></div>上林禁苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364574_comment'></div>层台累榭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364574_comment'></div>人君之丽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364574_comment'></div>而陛下宫垣不葺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364574_comment'></div>廊宇莫修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364574_comment'></div>置拾遗补阙之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364574_comment'></div>则前疑后承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364574_comment'></div>仰天俯地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364574_comment'></div>孰云尚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364574_comment'></div>创通贤招谏之匦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364574_comment'></div>则听声之鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364574_comment'></div>告善之旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364574_comment'></div>畴以懿兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364574_comment'></div>夫然后不登而高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364574_comment'></div>不行而远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364574_comment'></div>天降以瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364574_comment'></div>地升以符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364574_comment'></div>日月光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364574_comment'></div>风雨润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364574_comment'></div>庆云出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364574_comment'></div>神泉涌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364574_comment'></div>凤凰翔于庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364574_comment'></div>麒麟臻于囿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364574_comment'></div>云集雾散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364574_comment'></div>日至月书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364574_comment'></div>固不可得而言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364574_comment'></div>陛下犹固守冲挹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364574_comment'></div>深惟惕厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364574_comment'></div>以元默为神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364574_comment'></div>澹泊为德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364574_comment'></div>回圣虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364574_comment'></div>运全谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364574_comment'></div>采衢室之旧仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364574_comment'></div>酌明台之故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364574_comment'></div>因人之欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364574_comment'></div>不日而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364574_comment'></div>于是灵命孔彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364574_comment'></div>元心总集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364574_comment'></div>山开秘篆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364574_comment'></div>洛出祥图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364574_comment'></div>每缨冕同观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364574_comment'></div>轩墀共谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364574_comment'></div>则有曦车五色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364574_comment'></div>对玉匣而如迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364574_comment'></div>云盖三层。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364574_comment'></div>伴琼缄而不去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364574_comment'></div>岂非显见神物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364574_comment'></div>觉寤黎蒸者欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364574_comment'></div>可以昭报昊穹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364574_comment'></div>可以抑扬宗社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364574_comment'></div>明至德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364574_comment'></div>表至功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364574_comment'></div>阴阳不测之谓神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364574_comment'></div>应变不穷之谓圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364574_comment'></div>洋洋乎发育万物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364574_comment'></div>荡荡乎人无能名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1364574_comment'></div>尊号之来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364574_comment'></div>岂徒然而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1364574_comment'></div>圣母神皇乃不得已而从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364574_comment'></div>命有司膺大礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364574_comment'></div>秩群望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364574_comment'></div>怀百神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364574_comment'></div>配诸侯于四渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364574_comment'></div>视上公于五镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364574_comment'></div>百姓有罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364574_comment'></div>思与天下涤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1364574_comment'></div>一人有庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1364574_comment'></div>思与天下覃之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1364574_comment'></div>垂动钥之深思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1364574_comment'></div>降合钱之普泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1364574_comment'></div>凡百在宥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1364574_comment'></div>不知手之舞之足之蹈之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1364574_comment'></div>岂使女娲神化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1364574_comment'></div>仍参泰古之皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1364574_comment'></div>太姒徽音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1364574_comment'></div>独擅隆周之母而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1364574_comment'></div>微臣早沾扬历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1364574_comment'></div>亟奉恩荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1364574_comment'></div>惭拥肿之曲材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1364574_comment'></div>荷生成之大德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1364574_comment'></div>山涛者浑金之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1364574_comment'></div>魏国擢之以尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1364574_comment'></div>伊尹者饰玉之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1364574_comment'></div>殷朝待之于右相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1364574_comment'></div>在臣驽暗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1364574_comment'></div>远谢贤明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1364574_comment'></div>徼逢振拭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1364574_comment'></div>擢登左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1364574_comment'></div>陛下不以臣不肖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1364574_comment'></div>复使臣待罪元戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1364574_comment'></div>顾无平虏之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1364574_comment'></div>未荅破羌之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1364574_comment'></div>恭闻瑞典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1364574_comment'></div>载沐鸿私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1364574_comment'></div>幸属皇羲之代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1364574_comment'></div>欣承帝魁之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1364574_comment'></div>冕旒端拱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1364574_comment'></div>既不获接景前行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1364574_comment'></div>玉帛来朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1364574_comment'></div>又不获趋风后位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1364574_comment'></div>横行万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1364574_comment'></div>限中国以长城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1364574_comment'></div>悚踊一隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1364574_comment'></div>望东朝于西域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1364574_comment'></div>不任悦豫翘勤之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1364574_comment'></div>谨遣某官奉表称贺以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_230_1364574_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364606?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为韦右相贺平贼表</a><span class='authorDate'>（688年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14914, "初唐", "崔融", "poem_title_1364606")'>崔融</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364606_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364606'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364606'>臣某言。伏奉某月日递敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364606_comment'></div>逆贼等并已传首都市。幕庭拜受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364606_comment'></div>旌门宣告。凡预军司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364606_comment'></div>孰不庆悦。中贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364606_comment'></div>臣闻恶禽怪兽。有以彰普覆之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364606_comment'></div>乱臣逆子。不能损盛明之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364606_comment'></div>故三监作难。周王未寝于颂声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364606_comment'></div>七国为灾。汉帝克臻于刑措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364606_comment'></div>伏惟圣母神皇陛下象天之运。法地之安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364606_comment'></div>泽浸河海。光悬日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364606_comment'></div>以忠信为甲冑。以慈惠为干戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364606_comment'></div>所向无前。何人不服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364606_comment'></div>举神兵如电扫。破凶党若冰离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364606_comment'></div>数月妖氛。一朝清荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364606_comment'></div>斯实皇威远肃。圣化傍沾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364606_comment'></div>故能市不改肆。人皆安堵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364606_comment'></div>臣滥承天泽。忝预戎麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364606_comment'></div>闻逆命而增愤。听枭悬而累抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364606_comment'></div>庆快之情。倍百恒品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364606_comment'></div>不任悦豫之至。谨附某官奉表称贺以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364606_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1364606_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364576' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364576' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364576?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进洛图颂表</a><span class='authorDate'>（688年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14914, "初唐", "崔融", "poem_title_1364576")'>崔融</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364576_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364576'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364576'>臣某言。奉某年月日敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364576_comment'></div>令臣撰洛图颂。伏以陛下圣烈<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1364576", 1364576, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>丰懿</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364576_comment'></div>应期首出。珍符炳铄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364576_comment'></div>旷代䍐闻。虽皋繇歌虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364576_comment'></div>伯禹申叹。其或生于今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364576_comment'></div>尚不足以谈天。况臣涉学盖浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364576_comment'></div>揆才多陋。安可润色皇化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364576_comment'></div>对扬神休。窃读古文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364576_comment'></div>幽寻旧式。言大道者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364576_comment'></div>莫先于典诰。序以之生焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364576_comment'></div>美盛德者。莫近于诗什。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364576_comment'></div>颂以之成焉。其辞婉而微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364576_comment'></div>其事而要。今臣斟酌前训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364576_comment'></div>拟议鸿猷。述洛图颂一篇并序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364576_comment'></div>谨诣宣义门奉进。诚未能探索元奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364576_comment'></div>宪章经书。庶几竭肝胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364576_comment'></div>效尘露。增日月之末光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364576_comment'></div>偕天地而不朽。斯亦微臣之愿足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364576_comment'></div>臣拜手稽首冒颜以闻。死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364576_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1364576_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364577' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364577' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364577?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为朝集使于思言等请封中岳表</a><span class='authorDate'>（688年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14914, "初唐", "崔融", "poem_title_1364577")'>崔融</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364577_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364577'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364577'>臣某言。臣闻易有太极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364577_comment'></div>是生两仪。有父子焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364577_comment'></div>有君臣焉。道莫尊于三皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364577_comment'></div>皇合符于奕叶。德莫高于五帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364577_comment'></div>帝展事于云亭。礼莫盛于三王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364577_comment'></div>报功于岱畎。政莫隆于两汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364577_comment'></div>纪号于仙闾。皆所以省方观人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364577_comment'></div>增天益地。刻玉篆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364577_comment'></div>印金泥。激清流于渗漉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364577_comment'></div>翔仁风而萌动。然则业隆不封禅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364577_comment'></div>何以荅三灵。道备不巡游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364577_comment'></div>何以会万国。为人上者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364577_comment'></div>可不敬哉。中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364577_comment'></div>伏惟圣母神皇陛下宝命絪缊。元期肸蚃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364577_comment'></div>包混元而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364577", 1364577, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>建极</span>。宅造化而开阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364577_comment'></div>剖灵符于天。合至德于地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364577_comment'></div>渥泽浸润万物。恩光明悬四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364577_comment'></div>不言而含气风从。无为而流形日用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364577_comment'></div>允所谓荣镜绝代。弹压振古者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364577_comment'></div>臣闻古之圣王。受命者然后得封禅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364577_comment'></div>又云。功成道洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364577_comment'></div>符出乃封。又云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364577_comment'></div>致太平。必封禅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364577_comment'></div>今陛下获瑞铭于广武。得宝图于温洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364577_comment'></div>星连月合。云起风摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364577_comment'></div>上以拥神休。下以塞天望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364577_comment'></div>崇徽号。定都邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364577_comment'></div>文质再而复。正朔三而改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364577_comment'></div>义在得天。乃立天统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364577_comment'></div>非受命者。孰能臻兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364577_comment'></div>因时创宜。以顺制逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364577_comment'></div>建三庙。崇五茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364577_comment'></div>广太学以教冑子。开明堂而祀上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364577_comment'></div>彼东夷西戎。南蛮北狄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364577_comment'></div>殊方绝界。穷幽极远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364577_comment'></div>蠢然莫敢不来享。莫敢不来王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364577_comment'></div>非功成者。孰能臻兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364577_comment'></div>三阶平。万方晏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364577_comment'></div>岩廊无事。囹圄云空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364577_comment'></div>狱讼清而王风淳。礼乐和而人气乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364577_comment'></div>衢路有雁行之序。邑里得鹑居之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364577_comment'></div>五尺童儿。羞论霸道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364577_comment'></div>八十父老。不知帝力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364577_comment'></div>非道洽者。孰能臻兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364577_comment'></div>乾符总集。不召而自至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364577_comment'></div>坤瑞昭升。应图而合谍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364577_comment'></div>庆云出。神池涌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364577_comment'></div>毛宗扰。羽族驯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364577_comment'></div>树连理而麦两岐。□黄黍而□元秬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364577_comment'></div>匪朝伊夕。以时继年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364577_comment'></div>非符出者。孰能臻兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364577_comment'></div>命既受于天矣。功既成于人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364577_comment'></div>道已洽于古矣。符已出于今矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364577_comment'></div>若此者。非太平之效欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364577_comment'></div>可以升中名山。可以肆类上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364577_comment'></div>嵩高维岳。峻极于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364577_comment'></div>风雷所起。设险于畿甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364577_comment'></div>霜露所均。作镇于邦国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364577_comment'></div>虽复千八百处。未尝游玉女之台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364577_comment'></div>七十四家。不能幸仙人之洞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364577_comment'></div>区区汉武。止听三呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364577_comment'></div>汲汲晋炎。但諠群议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364577_comment'></div>臣等窃以为秘箓有云。中岳之神姓武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364577_comment'></div>天意若曰神皇其封中岳乎。藏纤纬以须时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364577_comment'></div>蓄符祥而待圣。显见神迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364577_comment'></div>觉寤黎蒸。天祚岳姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364577_comment'></div>必将封祀。封祀神岳者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364577_comment'></div>非陛下而谁。由是王公侯伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364577_comment'></div>日夕登封之奏。礼官博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364577_comment'></div>岁时符命之书。鸿儒硕学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364577_comment'></div>思献仪于野外。川后山祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364577_comment'></div>愿前驱于阙下。天人之望久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364577_comment'></div>陛下何得而辞哉。伏乞深惟至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364577_comment'></div>仰祗灵眷。傍稽瑞命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364577_comment'></div>俯顺<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_74_1364577", 1364577, "Clauses/148/Comments/0")'>氓歌</span>。龙驾帝服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364577_comment'></div>背河洛而上沂。星陈天行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364577_comment'></div>指轘嵩而东迈。石芝生而五色可以为盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364577_comment'></div>贝树长而三花可以为籍。埋玉报地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364577_comment'></div>燔柴告天。载巍巍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364577_comment'></div>扇翼翼。上以荅昊穹之储祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364577_comment'></div>下以副率土之欢心。永保鸿名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364577_comment'></div>长为称首。盛矣美矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364577_comment'></div>猗欤伟欤。臣等忝职外台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364577_comment'></div>受委方玉。宣太平之风化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364577_comment'></div>听古老之讴谣。望属车而未来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364577_comment'></div>思叫阍而至极。庶千年一会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364577_comment'></div>陛下垂不让之恩。使五载四朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364577_comment'></div>群臣有庆成之地。孰不幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364577_comment'></div>不胜悃款之至。谨诣朝堂奉表诚请以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364577_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_89_1364577_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

大名

<div class='label1' id='85090bee2b174e54a1fd3dea33473524_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("85090bee2b174e54a1fd3dea33473524");'><span id='85090bee2b174e54a1fd3dea33473524_link' 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>是年为魏州司功参军，有文。作品：《为魏州成使君贺白狼表》《为成魏州贺瑞雪庆云日抱戴表》<div id='poem_1364603' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364603' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_1364603_comment'></div>得令孟神符牒称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364603_comment'></div>某日得佐吏长寿乡单守中状称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364603_comment'></div>隆周长寿两乡界有白狼见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364603_comment'></div>臣等尝恐是虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364603_comment'></div>未敢即申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364603_comment'></div>因处分诸乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364603_comment'></div>若有见者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364603_comment'></div>辄令系取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364603_comment'></div>某日长寿乡致仕前游击将军上柱国朱佛儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364603_comment'></div>于长寿乡界内逢白狼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364603_comment'></div>驯狎无惧人意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364603_comment'></div>遂以绳络头系得随送者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364603_comment'></div>臣谨按瑞应图云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364603_comment'></div>白狼者金狼精也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364603_comment'></div>殷汤时衔钩入于庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364603_comment'></div>王者仁智明哲即至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364603_comment'></div>动准法度即见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364603_comment'></div>周宣王时见而犬戎服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364603_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下元期兆朕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364603_comment'></div>灵命氤氲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364603_comment'></div>物类有感而必通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364603_comment'></div>符祥不召而总集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364603_comment'></div>金精累烁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364603_comment'></div>鼓铸于阴阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364603_comment'></div>玉毳霜翘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364603_comment'></div>腾倚于郊甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364603_comment'></div>应时乃出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364603_comment'></div>野心狎而无惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364603_comment'></div>有道则游。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364603_comment'></div>徵故事于璇钤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364603_comment'></div>考异闻于玉册。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364603_comment'></div>明久长之益寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364603_comment'></div>重以陛下独尊三界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364603_comment'></div>高视四天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364603_comment'></div>身运明哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364603_comment'></div>动循法度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364603_comment'></div>既合周王之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364603_comment'></div>仍彰犬戎之服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364603_comment'></div>上元潜惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364603_comment'></div>佛儿来送。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364603_comment'></div>天尊若曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364603_comment'></div>陛下养众生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364603_comment'></div>其如二乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364603_comment'></div>善守其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364603_comment'></div>亦可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364603_comment'></div>谨寻令式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364603_comment'></div>唯合申台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364603_comment'></div>臣以尊号初加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364603_comment'></div>神聪显应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364603_comment'></div>守文不奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364603_comment'></div>恐爽灵心。<div -----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0ba18e575d984edb8a9821a72285fd01_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0ba18e575d984edb8a9821a72285fd01");'><span id='0ba18e575d984edb8a9821a72285fd01_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=690&endYear=690')">690年</a>　由魏州司功参军擢授著作佐郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=690&endYear=690')">690年9月</a>　本月，改国号为周，改元天授，发十道存抚使，李嗣真存抚河东，和其诗而送之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=691&endYear=692')">691-692年</a>　是年在著作佐郎任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=693&endYear=693')">693年</a>　在著作佐郎任。杨炯卒，为作祭文。作品：《祭杨盈川文》<br id='poem_sentence_1_1364604_comment'></div>五座列降神之府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364604_comment'></div>赫赫中国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364604_comment'></div>九筵开布政之宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364604_comment'></div>自轩皇肇制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364604_comment'></div>帝尧嗣作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364604_comment'></div>历虞夏而维新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364604_comment'></div>在殷周而克壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364604_comment'></div>斯皆尊祖配帝。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1364604_comment'></div>顺阴阳以班令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364604_comment'></div>降及有汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364604_comment'></div>颇采前章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364604_comment'></div>虽年惟屡丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364604_comment'></div>而日不暇给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364604_comment'></div>过此以往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364604_comment'></div>寂寥无声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364604_comment'></div>伏惟天册金轮圣神皇帝陛下兴复旧邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364604_comment'></div>光启新邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364604_comment'></div>万物睹而圣人作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364604_comment'></div>百宝用而神灵滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364604_comment'></div>远肃迩安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364604_comment'></div>功成道洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364604_comment'></div>泥金刻玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364604_comment'></div>已修中岳之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364604_comment'></div>乘鸾驾龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364604_comment'></div>更葺正阳之礼。<div href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=695&endYear=695')">695年</a>　在著作佐郎任。有文。作品：《代百官贺明堂成上礼表》《为百官贺雨请复膳表》《为百官贺千叶莲表》<div id='poem_1364605' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364605'
