</span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14914, "初唐", "崔融", "poem_title_1364605")'>崔融</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364605_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364605'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364605'>臣某以下文武官若干人等上言。臣等闻上帝居高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364605_comment'></div>悬太微之府。先王建国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364605_comment'></div>辟宗祀之堂。不有圣人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364605_comment'></div>谁其经始。伏惟天册金轮圣神皇帝陛下尊祖扬祢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364605_comment'></div>严禋之德再光。统天顺时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364605_comment'></div>布政之道尤急。亲纡睿思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364605_comment'></div>躬运元模。故能上合乾象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364605_comment'></div>下当坤策。柱将扶而已立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364605_comment'></div>石未凿而悬开。丹鷟踶甍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364605_comment'></div>似鸣岐而远至。苍虬绕栋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364605_comment'></div>疑出河而欲飞。神光熠耀于向晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364605_comment'></div>仙乐清泠而方昼。月惟孟夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364605_comment'></div>时属正阳。张文物于阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364605_comment'></div>震声名于宇县。圣皇戾止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364605_comment'></div>诸侯在列。穆穆焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364605_comment'></div>禺禺焉。交喜气于三灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364605_comment'></div>动欢心于万类者也。臣等进窥朝典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364605_comment'></div>既逢尝麦之辰。旋顾野诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364605_comment'></div>轻袭献芹之礼。谨上礼若干舆如别项。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364605_comment'></div>滋疏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1364605", 1364605, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>鹤鼎</span>。味劣鲜庖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364605_comment'></div>何以延萐莆之凉。契芝英之寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364605_comment'></div>无任丹恳之至。谨奉表称贺随进以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364605_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1364605_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364594' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364594' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364594?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为百官贺雨请复膳表</a><span class='authorDate'>（695年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14914, "初唐", "崔融", "poem_title_1364594")'>崔融</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364594_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364594'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364594'>臣某等文武官若干人言。臣等闻太平之代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364594_comment'></div>天地合而流津。至德之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364594_comment'></div>阴阳和而布泽。所以三农滋殖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364594_comment'></div>百姓阜安。伏惟天册金轮圣神皇帝陛下宝命絪缊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364594_comment'></div>元期肸蚃。包混元而建极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364594_comment'></div>宅造化而开阶。德教布濩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364594_comment'></div>仁声洋溢。增高益厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364594_comment'></div>己修中岳之仪。顺时班令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364594_comment'></div>更缉正阳之礼。近以少愆甘澍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364594_comment'></div>亲发至诚。怀宋景之一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364594_comment'></div>采殷汤之六事。德音才降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364594_comment'></div>灵心允协。捧瑶缄而风起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364594_comment'></div>迎宝字而星流。云不崇朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364594_comment'></div>复三千之药草。雨必以夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364594_comment'></div>通百亿之江河。遍高下而同沾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364594_comment'></div>在公私而并及。陈留雨谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364594_comment'></div>譬此非多。栎阳雨金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364594_comment'></div>方斯未重。邦国延有年之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364594_comment'></div>黎元罢望岁之忧。臣等中贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364594_comment'></div>伏愿陛下凝神保和。颐情养寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364594_comment'></div>复鲜庖之旧膳。进<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1364594", 1364594, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>鹤鼎</span>之常羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364594_comment'></div>使芝英有驻液之期。萐莆知送凉之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364594_comment'></div>则光天之下。率土之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364594_comment'></div>孰不欣戴。孰不幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364594_comment'></div>微臣等幸逢休运。预沐恩波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364594_comment'></div>混虞兽而同欢。比齐禽而累抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364594_comment'></div>无任悚荷之至。谨诣朝堂奉表称贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364594_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1364594_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364602' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364602' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364602?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为百官贺千叶瑞莲表</a><span class='authorDate'>（695年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14914, "初唐", "崔融", "poem_title_1364602")'>崔融</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364602_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364602'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364602'>臣某等文武官若干人言。伏奉恩旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364602_comment'></div>垂示臣等千叶瑞莲。观其绿裹红葩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364602_comment'></div>缃茎素萼。露摇珠点。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364602_comment'></div>霞拆金须。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364602", 1364602, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>百星</span>交映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364602_comment'></div>羽盖张而一色。万目齐明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364602_comment'></div>车轮合而千状。谓翔鸾之欲舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364602_comment'></div>若群鹓之并飞。峰形耸而半天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364602_comment'></div>石势蹲而临海。冲气积其下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364602_comment'></div>惠风流其上。服之可以登仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364602_comment'></div>采之可以驻寿。虽复释梵天王之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364602_comment'></div>千影离娄。善住天子之池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364602_comment'></div>双辉灿烂。校之今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364602_comment'></div>未可同年。臣等谨按华严经云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364602_comment'></div>莲花世界是卢舍那佛成道之国。一莲花有百亿国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364602_comment'></div>无量清净经云。无量清净佛七宝池中生莲花上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364602_comment'></div>夫莲花者。出尘离染。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364602_comment'></div>清净无瑕。有以见如来之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364602_comment'></div>有以察如来之法。道之行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364602_comment'></div>曾不徒然。伏惟天册金轮圣神皇帝现此妙身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364602_comment'></div>当兹巨瑞。符契冥合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364602_comment'></div>影响不差。有百亿国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364602_comment'></div>无量清净者。天意若曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364602_comment'></div>护苏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1364602", 1364602, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>蚁结</span>。默啜蜂飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364602_comment'></div>闻鼓鞞而革面。望旌旗而悬首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364602_comment'></div>指挥而边境获安。高枕而中国无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364602_comment'></div>风行电扫。纳噍类于百亿之区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364602_comment'></div>雾廓尘销。反游魂于清净之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364602_comment'></div>深仁所及。不亦宏哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364602_comment'></div>臣等滥奉朝恩。亲披瑞牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364602_comment'></div>非常之贶。旷古未闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364602_comment'></div>殊特之珍。历代一见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364602_comment'></div>手舞足蹈。倍百常情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364602_comment'></div>无任庆跃之至。谨诣朝堂奉表陈贺以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364602_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1364602_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=696&endYear=696')">696年7月</a>　本月，春官尚书、梁王武三思东征契丹，辟为掌书记，陈子昂、杜审言等作诗送之。有诗。作品：《留别杜审言并呈洛中旧友》<div id='poem_46383' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_46383_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_46383'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_46383'>斑鬓今为别，红颜昨共游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_46383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_46383'>年年春不待，处处酒相留。<div id='poem_sentence_1_46383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_46383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_46383'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_46383_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=696&endYear=696')">696年12月</a>　腊月，以著作佐郎行右史。时散官为朝散大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=696&endYear=696')">696年</a>　在著作佐郎任。有文。作品：《周封中岳碑》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年1月</a>　正月，幽、朔初平，梁王武三思召回，自幽州入都，陈子昂等又作诗送之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年1月</a>　一月或稍后，迁著作郎，仍兼右史内供奉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年5月</a>　在凤阁舍人任。武后令撰序，叙王氏代阀。作品：《王氏宝章集序》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年闰10月</a>　在凤阁舍人任。上议请不捐安西龟玆、于阗、疏勒、碎叶四镇，有文。作品：《拔四镇议》<div id='poem_1364616' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364616' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364616?labeling=true' target='_blank'>拔四镇议</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年闰10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14914, "初唐", "崔融", "poem_title_1364616")'>崔融</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364616_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364616'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364616'>议曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364616_comment'></div>北狄之为中国患者久哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364616_comment'></div>唐虞以上为獯鬻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364616_comment'></div>殷周之际曰猃狁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364616_comment'></div>西京东国有匈奴冒顿焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364616_comment'></div>当涂典午有乌丸鲜卑焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364616_comment'></div>拓跋世则蠕蠕猖狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364616_comment'></div>宇文朝则突厥恣睢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364616_comment'></div>斯皆名号因时而改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364616_comment'></div>种落与运而迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364616_comment'></div>五帝不能臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364616_comment'></div>三王不能制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364616_comment'></div>兵连祸结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364616_comment'></div>无代不有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364616_comment'></div>长策远算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364616_comment'></div>旷古莫闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364616_comment'></div>夫胡者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364616_comment'></div>北狄之总名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364616_comment'></div>其地南接燕赵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364616_comment'></div>北穷沙漠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364616_comment'></div>东接九夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364616_comment'></div>西界六戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364616_comment'></div>天性骄傲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364616_comment'></div>觇伺便隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364616_comment'></div>鸟飞兽走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364616_comment'></div>草转水移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364616_comment'></div>自言天地所生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364616_comment'></div>日月所置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364616_comment'></div>南有大汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364616_comment'></div>北有强胡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364616_comment'></div>更相驰突。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364616_comment'></div>至今陷溃者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364616_comment'></div>靡岁而宁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364616_comment'></div>汉兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364616_comment'></div>高皇以百万众窘于平城之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364616_comment'></div>国人羞之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364616_comment'></div>逮至武帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364616_comment'></div>患其如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364616_comment'></div>赫然发愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364616_comment'></div>肆志远略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364616_comment'></div>建元中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364616_comment'></div>使张骞始通西域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364616_comment'></div>既而列四郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364616_comment'></div>据两关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364616_comment'></div>以断匈奴右臂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364616_comment'></div>乃复度河湟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364616_comment'></div>筑令居塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364616_comment'></div>以绝南羌北交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364616_comment'></div>于是乘障塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364616_comment'></div>绝亭燧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364616_comment'></div>出长城数千里矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364616_comment'></div>于斯时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364616_comment'></div>承文景元默之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364616_comment'></div>国用富强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364616_comment'></div>太仓之粟相因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364616_comment'></div>水衡之钱贯朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364616_comment'></div>练兵选将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364616_comment'></div>深入穷追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364616_comment'></div>倾府库之财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364616_comment'></div>殚士马之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364616_comment'></div>行人使者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364616_comment'></div>岁月亭障。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364616_comment'></div>贰师骠骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364616_comment'></div>首尾关河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364616_comment'></div>饿虎未摧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364616_comment'></div>其国已耗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364616_comment'></div>馲驼既死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364616_comment'></div>其人亦殄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364616_comment'></div>乃至造皮币。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364616_comment'></div>算缗钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364616_comment'></div>税舟车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364616_comment'></div>榷酒酤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364616_comment'></div>夫岂不怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364616_comment'></div>深惟长久之计然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364616_comment'></div>匈奴于是乎孤特远窜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364616_comment'></div>羽檄不行焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364616_comment'></div>始孝武开西域之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364616_comment'></div>为置使者校尉领护之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364616_comment'></div>宣元哀平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364616_comment'></div>其道不替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_305_1364616_comment'></div>因以为乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_306_1364616_comment'></div>此天下之至虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_307_1364616_comment'></div>社稷之深忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_308_1364616_comment'></div>竟从燮议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_309_1364616_comment'></div>今宜日慎一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_310_1364616_comment'></div>虽休勿休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_311_1364616_comment'></div>采侯应不可之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_312_1364616_comment'></div>纳傅燮深虑之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_313_1364616_comment'></div>然后风为号令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_314_1364616_comment'></div>雷为折冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_315_1364616_comment'></div>缮甲兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_316_1364616_comment'></div>思将帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_317_1364616_comment'></div>上与天合德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_318_1364616_comment'></div>下与地合明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_319_1364616_comment'></div>中与人合心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_320_1364616_comment'></div>善战者不阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_321_1364616_comment'></div>如斯而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_322_1364616_comment'></div>拔旧安之四镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_323_1364616_comment'></div>委难制之两凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_324_1364616_comment'></div>求将来之端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_325_1364616_comment'></div>考已然之验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_326_1364616_comment'></div>伏念五六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_327_1364616_comment'></div>至于再三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_328_1364616_comment'></div>愚下固陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_329_1364616_comment'></div>知其不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_330_1364616_comment'></div>伏惟朝廷再三察焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_331_1364616_comment'></div>谨议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_332_1364616_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年</a>　在凤阁舍人任。因郭元振上《宝剑篇》，武后遍赐文学大臣，与李峤等和之，有诗。作品：《咏宝剑》<div id='poem_46382' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_46382' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/46382?labeling=true' target='_blank'>咏宝剑</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14914, "初唐", "崔融", "poem_title_46382")'>崔融</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_46382_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_46382'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(514, "poem_allusion_46382")'>一旦为龙</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2971, "poem_allusion_46382")'>风胡</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_46382_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_46382'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_46382'>宝剑出<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_46382", 46382, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>昆吾</span>，龟龙夹采珠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_46382_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_46382'>五精初献术，千户竞沦<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作论）</span>都。<div id='poem_sentence_1_46382_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_46382'>匣气冲牛斗，山形转辘轳。<div id='poem_sentence_2_46382_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_46382'>欲知天下贵，持此问<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作谢）</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2971, "poem_sentence_3_46382")'>风胡</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_46382_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_46382'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_46382_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年</a>　在凤阁舍人任。有文。作品：《唐西崇福寺怀素禅师碑》《为百官贺断狱甘露降表》《为宗监请停政事表》<div id='poem_1364598' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364598' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364598?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为百官贺断狱甘露降表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14914, "初唐", "崔融", "poem_title_1364598")'>崔融</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364598_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364598'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364598'>臣某等文武百官若干人言。一昨伏见御史中丞吉顼称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364598_comment'></div>某日承制。推法司断事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364598_comment'></div>恶逆者会赦不免。谋反者会赦从流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364598_comment'></div>主上以为轻重不当。陷人入罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364598_comment'></div>制曰。君亲无将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364598_comment'></div>将而必诛。安有忠孝同极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364598_comment'></div>而流罪异贯。若此者岂钦恤之意邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364598_comment'></div>旋命主司奏上沿革。谨按贞观律唯有十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364598_comment'></div>其捕亡断狱两卷。乃是永徽二年长孙无忌等奏加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364598_comment'></div>果非庭坚所制。百寮蒙瞽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364598_comment'></div>一朝开凿。圣鉴元通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364598_comment'></div>有如影响。自发德音之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364598_comment'></div>每夜触处有甘露降者。臣等中贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364598_comment'></div>臣等闻刑罚者人之鞭策。号令者国之舟车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364598_comment'></div>所以惩恶止奸。辅政助化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364598_comment'></div>故轩辕之为君也。设法而天下安乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364598_comment'></div>陶唐之为帝也。察令而天下昭明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364598_comment'></div>然则不令而诛。不教而杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364598_comment'></div>是虐人也。法不胜奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364598_comment'></div>刑不制罪。是陷人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364598_comment'></div>有以知悬之象魏。布以都鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364598_comment'></div>是谓禁人为非。铭之钟鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364598_comment'></div>铸之金石。是谓丕天之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364598_comment'></div>为人上者。可不务乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364598_comment'></div>若乃前主所是疏为律。后主所是疏为令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364598_comment'></div>事有不合于古。不务于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364598_comment'></div>则弛而更张。矫以归正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364598_comment'></div>正朔三而改。文质再而复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364598_comment'></div>王礼不相袭。帝乐不相沿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364598_comment'></div>夫何为乎。亦云适时而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364598_comment'></div>惟天册金轮圣神皇帝陛下躬明哲之性。秉淑圣之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364598_comment'></div>顺风雨以发生。乘雷电以震耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364598_comment'></div>推功天地。所以告成太室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364598_comment'></div>致孝祖考。所以宗祀明堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364598_comment'></div>陈宝鼎于帝庭。正土圭于王邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364598_comment'></div>能事毕。颂声兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364598_comment'></div>冤积之气不彰。刑残之尸复育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364598_comment'></div>断狱四百。愈鉴寐于淳源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364598_comment'></div>科条三千。尚劬劳于画象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364598_comment'></div>日者有司奏牍。议事不明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364598_comment'></div>大圣当枢。囚人轸虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364598_comment'></div>但臣之事主。犹子之事亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364598_comment'></div>父子则身体发肤。君臣则股肱元首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364598_comment'></div>出忠入孝。义在俱全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364598_comment'></div>履霜坚冰。法无异罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364598_comment'></div>曲礼垂教。子处洿宫之条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364598_comment'></div>大传立文。臣从潴室之坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364598_comment'></div>何以才经赦宥。顿隔刑书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364598_comment'></div>反逆首条而遂生。恶逆末坐而犹死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364598_comment'></div>下上簪履。颠倒衣裳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364598_comment'></div>遂使吏生淫巧。人无常禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364598_comment'></div>逆节所以时萌。凶党由其或在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364598_comment'></div>夫立杀止杀。制刑息刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364598_comment'></div>重其死然后生。峻其法然后禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364598_comment'></div>礼以齐君子。刑以齐小人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364598_comment'></div>非惟闻义而输忠。固亦知教而迁善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364598_comment'></div>斲雕为朴。自然登至道之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364598_comment'></div>墨幪赭衣。何必独上皇之代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364598_comment'></div>铨也法也。念兹在兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364598_comment'></div>昔者仲尼修春秋。乱臣贼子惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364598_comment'></div>梁靖撰七序。窃位素食惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364598_comment'></div>况我大君财成。上帝制作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364598_comment'></div>昭昭焉若日月之代明。累累焉似星辰之错行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364598_comment'></div>有典有则。是彝是训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364598_comment'></div>怀生幸生而有馀。群下瞻仰而不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364598_comment'></div>萧相国捃摭秦法。窥天无阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364598_comment'></div>杜武库参定汉章。蹐地失措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364598_comment'></div>诚可以垂后。诚可以达幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364598_comment'></div>至人无心。灵契昭于元极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364598_comment'></div>昊天有命。神物萃于休期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364598_comment'></div>巽风未行。甘露频降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364598_comment'></div>亦何止言善而星退。躬祷而云来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364598_comment'></div>夫其素液繁洒。芳滋丰溢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364598_comment'></div>丛骈六气之英。摇动二仪之粹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364598_comment'></div>匝园林而并润。溥郡邑而同沾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364598_comment'></div>汉宫无假于玉杯。魏殿不劳于琼爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364598_comment'></div>臣等谨按。甘露者美露也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364598_comment'></div>一名膏露。一名天酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364598_comment'></div>其凝如脂。其甘如饴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364598_comment'></div>盖神灵之精。仁瑞之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364598_comment'></div>稽命徵云。称谥正名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364598_comment'></div>则苇竹受甘露。孙氏图云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364598_comment'></div>王者和气茂。则降于草木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364598_comment'></div>食之寿。援神契云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364598_comment'></div>天子刑于四海。德洞沦溟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364598_comment'></div>则甘露降。鹖冠子曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364598_comment'></div>圣人之德。上及太清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364598_comment'></div>下及太宁。中及万灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364598_comment'></div>则膏露下。白武通云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364598_comment'></div>甘露之降。则百物无不盛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364598_comment'></div>陛下俯回冲眷。亲定律文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364598_comment'></div>必也正名。果符稽命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364598_comment'></div>是使孟坚持论。谈功德而未详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364598_comment'></div>抱朴裁书。称太平而不尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364598_comment'></div>上可以辅圣躬之寿。下可以延庶物之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364598_comment'></div>言之动天。一至于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364598_comment'></div>臣等庇荫昌运。接景清朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364598_comment'></div>常勉志于克家。每勤诚于报国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364598_comment'></div>恭闻大典。伏览殊祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364598_comment'></div>臣知拱极之尊。子识晞阳之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364598_comment'></div>无任抃跃之至。谨诣朝堂奉表称贺以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364598_comment'></div>仍请宣付所司。颁告遐迩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364598_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_102_1364598_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364610' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364610' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364610?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为宗监请停政事表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14914, "初唐", "崔融", "poem_title_1364610")'>崔融</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364610_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364610'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364610'>臣楚客言。臣闻古之圣君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364610_comment'></div>慎择贤佐。故轩辕得力牧而为五帝先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364610_comment'></div>夏后得咎繇而为三王祖。殷之盛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364610_comment'></div>伊尹格于皇天。姬之隆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364610_comment'></div>虢叔闻于上帝。斯皆应风云之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364610_comment'></div>依日月之光。社稷系以兴衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364610_comment'></div>时政由其轻重。粤若大周之有国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364610_comment'></div>天策金轮圣神皇帝提封千里。光宅四天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364610_comment'></div>道化淳醲。神功静默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364610_comment'></div>虽尧年无事。久闻童子之谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364610_comment'></div>而汉家用人。或取匈奴之笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364610_comment'></div>臣某中谢。臣疲骖强策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364610_comment'></div>卒无行地之功。决羽曾飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364610_comment'></div>终䍐冲天之望。今臣经术浅短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364610_comment'></div>才能朴略。言不足以补世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364610_comment'></div>行不足以励时。徒以枝叶微姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364610_comment'></div>葭莩末属。遂得拔擢泥滓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364610_comment'></div>骞翥云霄。食君厚禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364610_comment'></div>不能有所输报。受君殊宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364610_comment'></div>不能有所发明。茫然政途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364610_comment'></div>妨此贤路。外惭众口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364610_comment'></div>内愧诸心。朝廷亦何异舍陆而泛舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364610_comment'></div>胶柱而调瑟。当域中之有道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364610_comment'></div>岂天下之无人。尝深鼎覆之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364610_comment'></div>每切鼓妖之惧。臣之恳恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364610_comment'></div>非欲自保其身。臣之区区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364610_comment'></div>切虑上尘于国。今者契丹大剿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364610_comment'></div>默啜自来。六合大同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364610_comment'></div>四方向化。加以朔旦冬至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364610_comment'></div>鼎命维新。五星若连珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364610_comment'></div>二曜如合璧。谓宜退不肖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364610_comment'></div>进贤良。与天同休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364610_comment'></div>与人更始。又闻管夷吾有言曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364610_comment'></div>德义未明于朝。而使居尊位者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364610_comment'></div>则良臣不进也。功力未见于国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364610_comment'></div>而令处重禄者。则劳臣不劝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364610_comment'></div>臣有何德而居之。臣有何功而处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364610_comment'></div>臣虽至愚。敢忘先诫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364610_comment'></div>伏乞陛下察匹夫之志。思仲父之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364610_comment'></div>坦至公之方。宏灭私之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364610_comment'></div>羊叔子之辞开府。臣事君以忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364610_comment'></div>庾元规之让中书。君使臣以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364610_comment'></div>博求于众。广听于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364610_comment'></div>停臣检校夏官。辍臣平章政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364610_comment'></div>臣得避位清切。待罪上方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364610_comment'></div>罄竭单诚。庶几或济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364610_comment'></div>伏惟陛下容纳纤陋。鉴揆愚蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364610_comment'></div>使周勃无浃背之惭。虞邱有退身之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364610_comment'></div>则虽死之日。犹生之年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364610_comment'></div>无任悃款屏营之至。谨诣阙奉表陈情以闻云云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364610_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1364610_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=698&endYear=698')">698年</a>　在凤阁舍人任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=699&endYear=699')">699年</a>　在凤阁舍人任，姑系于此。<br /></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=700&endYear=700')">700年6月</a>　预修《三教珠英》。时改控鹤府为奉宸府，以张易之为令，引辞人阎朝等为供奉。武三思奏云易之弟昌宗是王子晋后身，辞人皆赋诗美之，崔融所作为绝唱。作品：《和梁王众传张光禄是王子晋后身》<div id='poem_46386' class='_poem'><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=700&endYear=700')">700年</a>　时天下禁屠宰，上议以为，此禁有三不可，非国家之大体，有文。作品：《断屠议》<div id='poem_1364615' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364615' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1364615'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364615'>议曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364615_comment'></div>春生秋杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364615_comment'></div>天之常道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364615_comment'></div>冬狩夏苗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364615_comment'></div>国之大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364615_comment'></div>豺祭兽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364615_comment'></div>獭祭鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364615_comment'></div>自然之理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364615_comment'></div>一乾豆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364615_comment'></div>二宾客。<div id='poem_sentence_16_1364615_comment'></div>人祇辑睦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364615_comment'></div>万王千帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364615_comment'></div>殊涂同归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364615_comment'></div>今若禁屠宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364615_comment'></div>断弋猎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364615_comment'></div>三驱莫行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364615_comment'></div>一切不许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364615_comment'></div>便恐违圣人之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1364615", 1364615, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>达训</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364615_comment'></div>紊明王之善经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364615_comment'></div>一不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364615_comment'></div>且如江南诸州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364615_comment'></div>乃以鱼为命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364615_comment'></div>河西诸国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364615_comment'></div>以肉为斋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364615_comment'></div>一朝禁止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364615_comment'></div>百姓劳弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364615_comment'></div>富者未革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364615_comment'></div>贫者难堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364615_comment'></div>二不可也。<div id='poem_sentence_37_1364615_comment'></div>家业倘失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364615_comment'></div>性命不全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364615_comment'></div>虽复日戮一人。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=702&endYear=702')">702年</a>　再迁凤阁舍人。上疏谏税关市。作品：《谏税关市疏》<div id='poem_1364613' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364613' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1364613'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364613'>伏见有司请税关市事条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364613_comment'></div>不限工商。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364613_comment'></div>但是行人尽税者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364613_comment'></div>臣谨按周礼九赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364613_comment'></div>其七曰关市之赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364613_comment'></div>窃惟市纵繁巧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364613_comment'></div>关通末游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364613_comment'></div>欲令此徒止抑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364613_comment'></div>所以咸增赋税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364613_comment'></div>臣谨商度今古。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1364613_comment'></div>谨件事迹如左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364613_comment'></div>伏惟圣旨择焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364613_comment'></div>往古之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364613_comment'></div>淳朴未散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364613_comment'></div>公田藉而不税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364613_comment'></div>关防讥而不征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364613_comment'></div>中代已来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364613_comment'></div>浇风骤进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364613_comment'></div>桑麻疲弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364613_comment'></div>稼穑辛勤。<div class='inline' "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>作巧</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364613_comment'></div>求径捷之欲速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364613_comment'></div>忘岁计之无馀。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364613_comment'></div>弊缊阙如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364613_comment'></div>饥寒猥臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364613_comment'></div>乱离斯瘼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364613_comment'></div>先王惩其若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364613_comment'></div>所以变古随时。<div id='poem_sentence_34_1364613_comment'></div>占末者增税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364613_comment'></div>夫关市之税者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364613_comment'></div>谓市及国门关门者也。<div id='poem_sentence_49_1364613_comment'></div>臣知其不可者一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364613_comment'></div>臣谨按易系称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364613_comment'></div>庖牺氏没。<div id='poem_sentence_54_1364613_comment'></div>致天下之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364613_comment'></div>聚天下之货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364613_comment'></div>交易而退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364613_comment'></div>奉顺天德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364613_comment'></div>理国安人之本也。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_300_1364613_comment'></div>惟陛下详之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1364613_comment'></div>必若师兴有费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_302_1364613_comment'></div>国储多窘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_303_1364613_comment'></div>即请倍算商客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_304_1364613_comment'></div>加敛平人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_305_1364613_comment'></div>如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_306_1364613_comment'></div>则国保富强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_307_1364613_comment'></div>人免忧惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_308_1364613_comment'></div>天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_309_1364613_comment'></div>臣知其不可者六也。<div id='poem_sentence_312_1364613_comment'></div>冒兹炎炽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_313_1364613_comment'></div>早朝宴坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_314_1364613_comment'></div>一日二日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364609_comment'></div>每岁立春立夏大暑立秋立冬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364609_comment'></div>常读五时令。<div class='inline' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364608?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为韦将军请上礼食表</a><span class='authorDate'>（706年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14914, "初唐", "崔融", "poem_title_1364608")'>崔融</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364608_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364608'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364608'>臣某言。臣闻坤德承天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364608_comment'></div>所以曲成万类。阴灵配日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364608_comment'></div>所以兼烛四方。故妫水佐虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364608_comment'></div>涂山翼夏。殷之兴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364608_comment'></div>有莘光其业。姬之盛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364608_comment'></div>太姒赞其功。用能家道以正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364608_comment'></div>国风兹始。伏惟陛下睿知神武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364608_comment'></div>文思聪明。光复丕基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364608_comment'></div>惟新宝运。包混元而建极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364608_comment'></div>体造化而开阶。流形日用而不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364608_comment'></div>含气风从而自乐。皇后坤维发祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364608_comment'></div>轩宫正位。黄云不散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364608_comment'></div>白气常流。玉玺载怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364608_comment'></div>椒涂以峻。洛书畴能谕其懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364608_comment'></div>河图不足纪其灵。外理克和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364608_comment'></div>内德惟茂。臣滥逢明圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364608_comment'></div>忝当姻戚。荣宠被于门庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364608_comment'></div>光耀生于道路。西京六族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364608_comment'></div>在昔何优。东国七家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364608_comment'></div>方今未重。鱼鳖咸若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364608_comment'></div>在品物而同欢。鸟兽率舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364608_comment'></div>顾微臣而倍跃。臣闻饮食之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364608_comment'></div>圣贤所贵。以奉君人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364608_comment'></div>以亲宗族。敢因斯义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364608_comment'></div>辄罄丹诚。伏望时降特恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364608_comment'></div>听臣上礼。虽玉饔珍味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364608_comment'></div>固无假于献芹。而臣下微心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364608_comment'></div>寔有同于倾藿。瞻言抃踊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364608_comment'></div>伏伫矜遂。无任悃款踊跃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364608_comment'></div>谨奉表陈情以闻。伏听敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364608_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1364608_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=706&endYear=706')">706年</a>　在国子司业、兼修国史任。时越州云门寺禅师道亮于西园问道，与贺知章等五人为法嗣，同心仰慕，请问禅心。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=706&endYear=706')">706年2月</a>　本月，已故密、亳州刺史郑仁恺制赠安州都督，为作碑。作品：《唐故密亳二州刺史赠安州都督郑公碑》<div id='poem_1364621' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364621' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364621?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故密亳二州刺史赠安州都督郑公碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（706年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14914, "初唐", "崔融", "poem_title_1364621")'>崔融</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364621_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364621'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364621'>公讳仁恺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364621_comment'></div>字仁恺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364621_comment'></div>郑者宗周之圻内国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364621_comment'></div>宣王封其弟友于咸林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364621_comment'></div>以国为姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364621_comment'></div>京兆□其都□至武公定平王东迁之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364621_comment'></div>晋郑焉依<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙八字）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364621_comment'></div>济前华后河食溱洧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364621_comment'></div>河南新郑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364621_comment'></div>是故今为荧阳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364621_comment'></div>我武公父子代为周司徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364621_comment'></div>诗人美之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364621_comment'></div>其诗曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364621_comment'></div>缁衣之宜兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364621_comment'></div>弊予又改为兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364621_comment'></div>□有司农□□汉有司农□□□□□□晋有司空袤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364621_comment'></div>洋洋乎良史书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364621_comment'></div>清风流于四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364621_comment'></div>盛德加于百代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364621_comment'></div>郁为天下甲族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364621_comment'></div>搢绅士大夫靡然到今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364621_comment'></div>犹鳞介之宗龟龙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364621_comment'></div>曾祖□育周议曹□□□□骑中□□□□□□守祖子裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364621_comment'></div>周毕王友大丞相府仓曹武泉郡太守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364621_comment'></div>父宏谅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364621_comment'></div>隋安定郡法曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364621_comment'></div>并列为君子之林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364621_comment'></div>称为英俊之□易其至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364621_comment'></div>知微而知章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364621_comment'></div>诗不云乎令闻□令望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364621_comment'></div>杨公四叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364621_comment'></div>远推□□之孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364621_comment'></div>杜侯五代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364621_comment'></div>复见神仙之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364621_comment'></div>公吸淳耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364621_comment'></div>滋灵液。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364621_comment'></div>因地美而芝兰生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364621_comment'></div>受天真而松柏茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364621_comment'></div>怀文抱质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364621_comment'></div>□□□方机思内潜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364621_comment'></div>□□外□拔自弱冠□□□□□□艰□殆将灭性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364621_comment'></div>属隋氏爽驭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364621_comment'></div>海水群飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364621_comment'></div>衣冠荡析。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364621_comment'></div>既乱离而瘼矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364621_comment'></div>礼乐逃散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364621_comment'></div>争携持而去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364621_comment'></div>圣唐载造区夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364621_comment'></div>削平宇宙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364621_comment'></div>□道焚林求贤命职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364621_comment'></div>起家补<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙八字）</span>宗卫录事参军拜□□子通事舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364621_comment'></div>迁詹事府主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364621_comment'></div>汉邸与邹枚并游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364621_comment'></div>邺园与应刘方驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364621_comment'></div>转豳州三水同州蒲城二县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364621_comment'></div>君述职二城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364621_comment'></div>推明三辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364621_comment'></div>覈为政□□□□养□□□辟土植谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364621_comment'></div>夏长秋成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364621_comment'></div>市无堕游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364621_comment'></div>家安农业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364621_comment'></div>鱼菜不乏食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364621_comment'></div>毛米无所□□□望风□□□□党闻名而自化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364621_comment'></div>秩满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364621_comment'></div>迁莱州长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364621_comment'></div>是时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364621_comment'></div>青邱负阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364621_comment'></div>沧海扬波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364621_comment'></div>乃眷行师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364621_comment'></div>深惟利涉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364621_comment'></div>制命公为造船使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364621_comment'></div>赤马黄龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364621_comment'></div>万艘千轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364621_comment'></div>成之不日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364621_comment'></div>望之如云<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙十字）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364621_comment'></div>以西候多虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364621_comment'></div>边寄为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364621_comment'></div>制授公□州都督府司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364621_comment'></div>驰驿之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364621_comment'></div>都督崔馀庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364621_comment'></div>绝俗之士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364621_comment'></div>每推公清心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364621_comment'></div>谈不容口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364621_comment'></div>属高宗升中岱岳预陪<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙十字）</span>寻□□州长史□之□□旧壤湫□□□□咨□诉□□□□□乃□□占星离疆画野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364621_comment'></div>得郊原之爽垲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364621_comment'></div>当水陆之要冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364621_comment'></div>城邑洞开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364621_comment'></div>闾阎对出<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙十二字）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364621_comment'></div>权授使持节密州诸军事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364621_comment'></div>守密州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364621_comment'></div>□叶推良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364621_comment'></div>门归通德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364621_comment'></div>有同衣锦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364621_comment'></div>时论荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364621_comment'></div>居无何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364621_comment'></div>迁使持节亳州诸军事亳州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364621_comment'></div>传车骖驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364621_comment'></div>鼓吹旌旗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364621_comment'></div>故人不敢私恩□□□子□□相名□乡□□□国霸□□□大行惠化丰洽□乎时礼云及年病相成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364621_comment'></div>可以致政于君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364621_comment'></div>可以传事于子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364621_comment'></div>诣阙上书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364621_comment'></div>乞辞荣秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364621_comment'></div>优制许焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364621_comment'></div>从高志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364621_comment'></div>婆娑田□夭㑥邱坟始鸠杖而□□俄□衣而□□□□□元□岁□□□九月□□朔廿五日□□遘疾薨于东都惠训里第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364621_comment'></div>享年七十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364621_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364621_comment'></div>惟公五山之精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364621_comment'></div>六金之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364621_comment'></div>大□所成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364621_comment'></div>刜钟无声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364621_comment'></div>生而异状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364621_comment'></div>幼而殊□□□□□成□□□□□信发□□□□清机虚冲默体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364621_comment'></div>言出乎口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364621_comment'></div>应而莫违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364621_comment'></div>道存乎身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364621_comment'></div>酌而罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364621_comment'></div>延颈者日有所得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364621_comment'></div>倾耳者日有所闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364621_comment'></div>节于损已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364621_comment'></div>丰于济物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364621_comment'></div>四践□□二登邑宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364621_comment'></div>三为别<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙十一字）</span>朝□夫学始于周孔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364621_comment'></div>中于老庄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364621_comment'></div>终于释教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364621_comment'></div>故能全耳目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364621_comment'></div>逸形神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364621_comment'></div>兀然体命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364621_comment'></div>油然合道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364621_comment'></div>彼苍不仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364621_comment'></div>歼我明悊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364621_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364621_comment'></div>以其年十一月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364621_comment'></div>与夫人合葬<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙十字）</span>平原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364621_comment'></div>礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364621_comment'></div>垂拱二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364621_comment'></div>贝州父老乃相与而谋曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364621_comment'></div>自州辞骥足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364621_comment'></div>及野送龙⿰<span class='inlineComment2'>（车春）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364621_comment'></div>缠慕百城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364621_comment'></div>行淹一纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364621_comment'></div>昔年草莽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364621_comment'></div>閒桃李而<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙十字）</span>两邑<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙九字）</span>德逾芳神其如在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364621_comment'></div>咸恐栾公之社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364621_comment'></div>蓬渚何常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364621_comment'></div>武侯之祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364621_comment'></div>桑田且变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364621_comment'></div>广祈时彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364621_comment'></div>奉赞徽音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364621_comment'></div>乃建丰碑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364621_comment'></div>式扬清德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364621_comment'></div>其碑先寘于<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙十字）</span>临<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙八字）</span>纪绩刊碑情深于即事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364621_comment'></div>未有居诸逾于十载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364621_comment'></div>犹结去思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364621_comment'></div>人吏隔于存亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364621_comment'></div>仍崇颂记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364621_comment'></div>虽周人缅怀于邵伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364621_comment'></div>未是过<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙十六字）</span>豫郡□□□□□□之镇荆州千年堕泪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364621_comment'></div>夫人清河郡君房氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364621_comment'></div>隋司隶刺史皇朝赠徐州都督临淄定公之孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364621_comment'></div>太尉<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙二十九字）</span>公特所钟爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364621_comment'></div>每谓亲族曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364621_comment'></div>我女实贤明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364621_comment'></div>尝退朝之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364621_comment'></div>时与参谋政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364621_comment'></div>及御车有典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364621_comment'></div>结镜言归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364621_comment'></div>芬若椒<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙二十三字）</span>匡夫□范训子知方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364621_comment'></div>博综书林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364621_comment'></div>深明觉道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364621_comment'></div>性纯孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364621_comment'></div>初丁公忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364621_comment'></div>哀毁踰礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364621_comment'></div>乃表奏男智度女光严出家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364621_comment'></div>以申追福<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙二十四字）</span>悲□今日西阶之葬应天皇帝纂尧兴运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364621_comment'></div>嗣夏配天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364621_comment'></div>遽覃锡类之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364621_comment'></div>特降追荣之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364621_comment'></div>神龙二年二月一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364621_comment'></div>制赠公<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙十三字）</span>军事安<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙七字）</span>之赠鸿恩被于九京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1364621_comment'></div>高密邓禹之封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364621_comment'></div>盛烈光于千载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1364621_comment'></div>有子十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364621_comment'></div>长曰爱客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364621_comment'></div>万州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364621_comment'></div>赠□州刺史□□□□朝<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙二十字）</span>朗州刺□□子真客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364621_comment'></div>中散大夫晋州临汾令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364621_comment'></div>次子智度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364621_comment'></div>京懿德寺僧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364621_comment'></div>次子固忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1364621_comment'></div>定潞许三州刺史少府少□□□□□二□□□□书□部侍郎次子慈明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1364621_comment'></div>赵□□□□□□卿曹州刺□次子信卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1364621_comment'></div>左屯卫长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1364621_comment'></div>八龙齐骋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1364621_comment'></div>六凤群飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1364621_comment'></div>读先圣之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1364621_comment'></div>行诸侯之孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1364621_comment'></div>潘中郎之茹泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1364621_comment'></div>顾慕修埏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1364621_comment'></div>□内史之衔□□□大□灵衣曳曳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1364621_comment'></div>容驾迟迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1364621_comment'></div>当松柏之□□在桑榆之暮时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1364621_comment'></div>元阙□□不复睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1364621_comment'></div>阴堂闭兮从此辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1364621_comment'></div>乃作铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1364621_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_206_1364621'>大哉宣后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1364621_comment'></div>诗歌中兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1364621_comment'></div>武公载德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1364621_comment'></div>缁衣是称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1364621_comment'></div>乃作卿士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1364621_comment'></div>良哉股肱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1364621_comment'></div>玉鈜金干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1364621_comment'></div>□涌□蒸盛德必祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1364621_comment'></div>信而有徵<span class='inlineComment2'>（其一）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1364621_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_215_1364621'>惟岳降神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1364621_comment'></div>生甫及申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1364621_comment'></div>□□纯嘏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1364621_comment'></div>文质彬彬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1364621_comment'></div>道光邦国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1364621_comment'></div>行重彝伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1364621_comment'></div>廊庙之宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1364621_comment'></div>社稷之臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（其二）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1364621_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_223_1364621'>肃肃端士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1364621_comment'></div>宦成两宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1364621_comment'></div>英英时彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1364621_comment'></div>□□□同舞鸾驯雉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1364621_comment'></div>□□返风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1364621_comment'></div>太邱贲德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1364621_comment'></div>密贱推功<span class='inlineComment2'>（其三）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1364621_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_230_1364621'>魏重题舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1364621_comment'></div>汉隆□□□□□轼三居展骥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1364621_comment'></div>鳌川波静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1364621_comment'></div>鸟城风被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1364621_comment'></div>楛矢东来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1364621_comment'></div>白环西暨<span class='inlineComment2'>（其四）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1364621_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_236_1364621'>按节海沂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1364621_comment'></div>分符谯沛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1364621_comment'></div>明明良牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1364621_comment'></div>帝庭称最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1364621_comment'></div>迁□兽威□□□□一变浇俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1364621_comment'></div>翳公是赖<span class='inlineComment2'>（其五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1364621_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_242_1364621'>岁穷钟漏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1364621_comment'></div>日运□□□□□□广德悬车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1364621_comment'></div>方寻三略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1364621_comment'></div>言从二疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1364621_comment'></div>俄悲梦奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1364621_comment'></div>忽怆楹书<span class='inlineComment2'>（其六）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1364621_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_248_1364621'>汉封乐毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1364621_comment'></div>周祀庭坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1364621_comment'></div>皇矣圣作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1364621_comment'></div>畴德旌贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1364621_comment'></div>昭锡□□□□□□滕公之室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1364621_comment'></div>原氏之阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1364621_comment'></div>棠阴一谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1364621_comment'></div>堕泪千年<span class='inlineComment2'>（其七阙三字）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1364621_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_256_1364621'>兮谓盛德遵释老兮宪孔墨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1364621_comment'></div>孝于家兮忠于国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1364621_comment'></div>人之英兮士之则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1364621_comment'></div>朱鸟南兮元武北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1364621_comment'></div>日翳翳兮泉门黑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1364621_comment'></div>□冥冥兮□□□翠□□□丹字刻<span class='inlineComment2'>（其八）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_261_1364621_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=706&endYear=706')">706年</a>　春夏间，眉州刺史苏味道迁益州大都督府长史，未行而卒，终年五十八。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=706&endYear=706')">706年5月9日</a>　此日，修成《则天实录》三十卷，赐物五百段，玺书褒美。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=706&endYear=706')">706年</a>　数日后，撰文，用思精苦，遂发病卒，年五十四。赠卫州刺史，谥曰文。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
绵阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5af7971a7ded476097c9778973813812_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5af7971a7ded476097c9778973813812");'><span id='5af7971a7ded476097c9778973813812_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=700&endYear=700')">700年</a>，48岁</div><div id='5af7971a7ded476097c9778973813812' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，坐忤张昌宗意，贬绵州魏城县令。文散官为朝散大夫。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>是年有文。作品：《贺赦表》<div id='poem_1364596' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364596' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364596?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺赦表</a><span class='authorDate'>（700年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14914, "初唐", "崔融", "poem_title_1364596")'>崔融</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364596_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364596'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364596'>臣某言。臣伏奉久视元年十月十日墨制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364596_comment'></div>以一月为正。大赦天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364596_comment'></div>服周之冕。衣冠混于无外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364596_comment'></div>行夏之时。正朔覃于有截。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364596_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下天地合德。历数在躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364596_comment'></div>交日月于龙躔。会风云于凤纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364596_comment'></div>取新之化。首出于九皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364596_comment'></div>除旧之恩。曲成于庶类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364596_comment'></div>加以载怀孝享。肃事天田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364596_comment'></div>休声动于万国。盛礼悬于百代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364596_comment'></div>凡在形气。孰不昭苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364596_comment'></div>微臣庆偶时来。荣沾日用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364596_comment'></div>同草树而知乐。类鸟兽而增欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364596_comment'></div>迹虽限于一隅。心每驰于双阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364596_comment'></div>抃舞昌运。倍百恒情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364596_comment'></div>不任屏营之至。谨附贺正使某官奉表称贺以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364596_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1364596_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

金华

-----title
宜春

-----title
蕲春
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c2bad795827140c987ac5bd437269b4b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c2bad795827140c987ac5bd437269b4b");'><span id='c2bad795827140c987ac5bd437269b4b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=706&endYear=706')">706年</a>，54岁</div><div id='c2bad795827140c987ac5bd437269b4b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=706&endYear=706')">706年</a>　寒食，与宋之问等相继至蕲州黄梅县之临江驿，之问题诗并寄赠，和之。作品：《和宋之问寒食题黄梅临江驿》<span class='inlineComment2'>（“间”误，应为“问”字。）</span><div id='poem_46381' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_46381' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/46381?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和宋之问寒食题黄梅临江驿</a><span class='authorDate'>（706年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14914, "初唐", "崔融", "poem_title_46381")'>崔融</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_46381_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_46381'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_46381'>春分自淮北，寒食渡江南。<div id='poem_sentence_0_46381_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_46381'>忽见浔阳水，疑是宋家潭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_46381_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_46381'>明主阍难叫，孤臣逐未堪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_46381_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_46381'>遥思故园陌，桃李正<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_46381", 46381, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>酣酣</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_46381_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_46381'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_46381_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
九江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b34e366d85814511bbd21767f28037cf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b34e366d85814511bbd21767f28037cf");'><span id='b34e366d85814511bbd21767f28037cf_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=706&endYear=706')">706年</a>，54岁</div><div id='b34e366d85814511bbd21767f28037cf' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=706&endYear=706')">706年</a>　同年秋，召为国子司业。经江州虎溪太平兴龙寺即东林寺，题诗。作品：《游东林寺》<br /></div>
